A suggestion for some, over polite, young waiters: don't ask too quickly to change your plate, while guests enjoy the food in peace. A little more distance will be fine and shows professionalism.

Also here the dinner have good quality, si special and delicious.

The spacious view from the room and clubroom are particularly beautiful and varied because of the ebb and flow. On our last day we saw the full rainbow, really beautiful.

The hotel is easily accessible and from here all attractions and business visits are within easy reach.

Finally, the hotel is rightfully worthy of 5 stars. We can warmly recommend this hotel to everyone. We look forward to our next stay here.

msg:Because it is a newly opened hotel, I thought it would be good for word of mouth, and the service and facilities should be good. Who knows, on the contrary, it is also a rare and poor experience for so many years. There are mainly the following points to complain, I hope to give some tips to parents who are choosing a hotel:
1. We are a family of four traveling, old and young. We have booked two rooms. We hope to arrange the same floor when we check in, so that we can take care of them easily. The front desk and the duty manager insisted that the room was full and could not be arranged. There are two rooms separated by four floors.
The whole floor where the second room was located smelled of smoke, and it was more obvious in the room. We asked for a room change, but we didn't agree at first, only to provide an air purifier. Only after strong request and negotiation did we agree to change rooms.
At this time, I was surprised. I just said that the room was full, and now there is room to spare? After further communication, I suddenly realized: they do have vacant rooms, but they have to reserve them for "pre-arrival" guests. I was puzzled. I also pre-arrived. Compared with the guests who haven't checked in yet, we still arrive first. There's always a first come first! Is it because we are the customers who purchased the package and are different from ordinary customers?
Again, because we didn't say in advance that we wanted a similar room. I just wanted to ask, is it incomprehensible for a family to travel and live in similar rooms according to normal logic, at least on the same floor? What is the basis for leaving empty rooms to the so-called "pre-arrival" guests and not assigning them to us?
Sure enough, in the end, under what they called "difficult" deployment, they were given two more rooms on the same floor.
This process is too tortuous and energy-consuming to negotiate, which makes me strongly feel the weakness as a consumer, the asymmetry of hotel information, and the issue of integrity. If you don't insist, you may not be able to defend your rights.
2. Because we arrived by plane at 10:00 at night, it was almost 1:00 in the morning after changing the room. After the change, the two rooms still smelled of smoke. I haven't slept well all night, not to mention the elderly and children. Because of the trouble of changing rooms, we asked the front desk to deal with the smoke smell in the room in the early morning, hoping to deal with it before we went out to play. After returning to the room after 8 o'clock in the evening, I found that the smoke smell in one of the rooms was difficult to remove (after I came back, I asked the waiter to come in and spray the air freshener once, and the smoke smell came out again after dissipating). It is impossible, only to change rooms again.
The hotel is indeed non-smoking throughout the area, but there are no effective measures to supervise the guests not to smoke, and there is no good way to get rid of the smoke smell in the room. The probability of staying in a smoke-smelling room is really high, and it is the guests who suffer.
3. The package of the hotel we purchased included fruits and afternoon tea, which is far from the package of the five-star hotel I have experienced before. There are three small pieces of fruit, and afternoon tea cannot be reserved and delivered during the travel time of the guests. room. Such packages are useless.
4. Small complaints: The first photo is of stains on the sofa, and the bathroom was not cleaned in time. The cup is cracked. There is no full-length mirror in the suite.
